2019-12-04 01:27:06.209 -06:00 [INF] Executed DbCommand (74ms) [Parameters=[@__id_0='30'], CommandType='"Text"', CommandTimeout='30']
SELECT TOP(2) [x].[Name], [x].[Owner], [x].[Amount], [x].[CreationDate], [x].[BudgetId], [x].[UserId], CASE
    WHEN (
        SELECT CASE
            WHEN EXISTS (
                SELECT 1
                FROM [Expenses] AS [e]
                WHERE [x].[BudgetId] = [e].[UserBudgetBudgetId])
            THEN CAST(1 AS BIT) ELSE CAST(0 AS BIT)
        END
    ) = 1
    THEN [x].[Amount] - (
        SELECT SUM([y].[Amount])
        FROM [Expenses] AS [y]
        WHERE [x].[BudgetId] = [y].[UserBudgetBudgetId]
    ) ELSE 0E0
END AS [Balance]
FROM [Budgets] AS [x]
WHERE ([x].[BudgetId] = @__id_0) AND ([x].[IsDeleted] = 0)
ORDER BY [x].[BudgetId]
2019-12-04 01:27:06.295 -06:00 [INF] Executed DbCommand (85ms) [Parameters=[@__id_0='30'], CommandType='"Text"', CommandTimeout='30']
SELECT [x.Expenses].[IdExpense], [x.Expenses].[Amount], [x.Expenses].[Category], [x.Expenses].[DateAdded], [x.Expenses].[Name], [x.Expenses].[Notes], [x.Expenses].[UserBudgetBudgetId], [x.Expenses].[UserId], [t].[BudgetId]
FROM [Expenses] AS [x.Expenses]
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT TOP(1) [x0].[BudgetId]
    FROM [Budgets] AS [x0]
    WHERE ([x0].[BudgetId] = @__id_0) AND ([x0].[IsDeleted] = 0)
    ORDER BY [x0].[BudgetId]
) AS [t] ON [x.Expenses].[UserBudgetBudgetId] = [t].[BudgetId]

SELECT TOP(2) [x].[Name], [x].[Owner], [x].[Amount], [x].[CreationDate], [x].[BudgetId], [x].[UserId], CASE
    WHEN (
        SELECT CASE
            WHEN EXISTS (
                SELECT 1
                FROM [Expenses] AS [e]
                WHERE [x].[BudgetId] = [e].[UserBudgetBudgetId])
            THEN CAST(1 AS BIT) ELSE CAST(0 AS BIT)
        END
    ) = 1
    THEN [x].[Amount] - (
        SELECT SUM([y].[Amount])
        FROM [Expenses] AS [y]
        WHERE [x].[BudgetId] = [y].[UserBudgetBudgetId]
    ) ELSE 0E0
END AS [Balance]
FROM [Budgets] AS [x]
WHERE ([x].[BudgetId] = @__id_0) AND ([x].[IsDeleted] = 0)
ORDER BY [x].[BudgetId]

SELECT TOP(2) [x].[Name], [x].[Owner], [x].[Amount], [x].[CreationDate], [x].[BudgetId], [x].[UserId], CASE
    WHEN (
        SELECT CASE
            WHEN EXISTS (
                SELECT 1
                FROM [Expenses] AS [e]
                WHERE [x].[BudgetId] = [e].[UserBudgetBudgetId])
            THEN CAST(1 AS BIT) ELSE CAST(0 AS BIT)
        END
    ) = 1
    THEN [x].[Amount] - (
        SELECT SUM([y].[Amount])
        FROM [Expenses] AS [y]
        WHERE [x].[BudgetId] = [y].[UserBudgetBudgetId]
    ) ELSE 0E0
END AS [Balance]
FROM [Budgets] AS [x]
WHERE ([x].[BudgetId] = @__id_0) AND ([x].[IsDeleted] = 0)
ORDER BY [x].[BudgetId]

FROM [Expenses] AS [x.Expenses]

SELECT TOP(2) [x].[Name], [x].[Owner], [x].[Amount], [x].[CreationDate], [x].[BudgetId], [x].[UserId], CASE
    WHEN (
        SELECT CASE
            WHEN EXISTS (
                SELECT 1
                FROM [Expenses] AS [e]
                WHERE [x].[BudgetId] = [e].[UserBudgetBudgetId])
            THEN CAST(1 AS BIT) ELSE CAST(0 AS BIT)
        END
    ) = 1
    THEN [x].[Amount] - (
        SELECT SUM([y].[Amount])
        FROM [Expenses] AS [y]
        WHERE [x].[BudgetId] = [y].[UserBudgetBudgetId]
    ) ELSE 0E0

SELECT TOP(2) [x].[Name], [x].[Owner], [x].[Amount], [x].[CreationDate], [x].[BudgetId], [x].[UserId], CASE
    WHEN (
        SELECT CASE
            WHEN EXISTS (
                SELECT 1
                FROM [Expenses] AS [e]
                WHERE [x].[BudgetId] = [e].[UserBudgetBudgetId])
            THEN CAST(1 AS BIT) ELSE CAST(0 AS BIT)
        END
    ) = 1
    THEN [x].[Amount] - (
        SELECT SUM([y].[Amount])
        FROM [Expenses] AS [y]
        WHERE [x].[BudgetId] = [y].[UserBudgetBudgetId]
    ) ELSE 0E0
END AS [Balance]
FROM [Budgets] AS [x]
WHERE ([x].[BudgetId] = @__id_0) AND ([x].[IsDeleted] = 0)
ORDER BY [x].[BudgetId]

SELECT TOP(2) [x].[Name], [x].[Owner], [x].[Amount], [x].[CreationDate], [x].[BudgetId], [x].[UserId], CASE
    WHEN (
        SELECT CASE
            WHEN EXISTS (
                SELECT 1
                FROM [Expenses] AS [e]
                WHERE [x].[BudgetId] = [e].[UserBudgetBudgetId])
            THEN CAST(1 AS BIT) ELSE CAST(0 AS BIT)
        END
    ) = 1
    THEN [x].[Amount] - (
        SELECT SUM([y].[Amount])
        FROM [Expenses] AS [y]
        WHERE [x].[BudgetId] = [y].[UserBudgetBudgetId]
    ) ELSE 0E0
END AS [Balance]
FROM [Budgets] AS [x]
WHERE ([x].[BudgetId] = @__id_0) AND ([x].[IsDeleted] = 0)
ORDER BY [x].[BudgetId]

SELECT TOP(2) [x].[Name], [x].[Owner], [x].[Amount], [x].[CreationDate], [x].[BudgetId], [x].[UserId], CASE
    WHEN (
        SELECT CASE
            WHEN EXISTS (
                SELECT 1
                FROM [Expenses] AS [e]

        END
    ) = 1
    THEN [x].[Amount] - (
        SELECT SUM([y].[Amount])
        FROM [Expenses] AS [y]
        WHERE [x].[BudgetId] = [y].[UserBudgetBudgetId]
    ) ELSE 0E0
END AS [Balance]
FROM [Budgets] AS [x]
WHERE ([x].[BudgetId] = @__id_0) AND ([x].[IsDeleted] = 0)

SELECT TOP(2) [x].[Name], [x].[Owner], [x].[Amount], [x].[CreationDate], [x].[BudgetId], [x].[UserId], CASE

        END

END AS [Balance]

    WHEN (
        SELECT CASE
            WHEN EXISTS (
                SELECT 1
                FROM [Expenses] AS [e]
                WHERE [x].[BudgetId] = [e].[UserBudgetBudgetId])

SELECT TOP(2) [x].[Name], [x].[Owner], [x].[Amount], [x].[CreationDate], [x].[BudgetId], [x].[UserId], CASE
    WHEN (
        SELECT CASE
            WHEN EXISTS (
                SELECT 1
                FROM [Expenses] AS [e]
                WHERE [x].[BudgetId] = [e].[UserBudgetBudgetId])
            THEN CAST(1 AS BIT) ELSE CAST(0 AS BIT)
        END
    ) = 1
    THEN [x].[Amount] - (
        SELECT SUM([y].[Amount])
        FROM [Expenses] AS [y]
        WHERE [x].[BudgetId] = [y].[UserBudgetBudgetId]
    ) ELSE 0E0
END AS [Balance]
FROM [Budgets] AS [x]
WHERE ([x].[BudgetId] = @__id_0) AND ([x].[IsDeleted] = 0)
ORDER BY [x].[BudgetId]

SELECT TOP(2) [x].[Name], [x].[Owner], [x].[Amount], [x].[CreationDate], [x].[BudgetId], [x].[UserId], CASE
    WHEN (
        SELECT CASE
            WHEN EXISTS (
                SELECT 1
                FROM [Expenses] AS [e]
                WHERE [x].[BudgetId] = [e].[UserBudgetBudgetId])

        END
    ) = 1

        FROM [Expenses] AS [y]
        WHERE [x].[BudgetId] = [y].[UserBudgetBudgetId]
    ) ELSE 0E0
END AS [Balance]
FROM [Budgets] AS [x]
WHERE ([x].[BudgetId] = @__id_0) AND ([x].[IsDeleted] = 0)

SELECT TOP(2) [x].[Name], [x].[Owner], [x].[Amount], [x].[CreationDate], [x].[BudgetId], [x].[UserId], CASE
    WHEN (
        SELECT CASE
            WHEN EXISTS (
                SELECT 1
                FROM [Expenses] AS [e]
                WHERE [x].[BudgetId] = [e].[UserBudgetBudgetId])
            THEN CAST(1 AS BIT) ELSE CAST(0 AS BIT)
        END
    ) = 1
    THEN [x].[Amount] - (
        SELECT SUM([y].[Amount])
        FROM [Expenses] AS [y]
        WHERE [x].[BudgetId] = [y].[UserBudgetBudgetId]
    ) ELSE 0E0
END AS [Balance]
FROM [Budgets] AS [x]
WHERE ([x].[BudgetId] = @__id_0) AND ([x].[IsDeleted] = 0)
ORDER BY [x].[BudgetId]

SELECT TOP(2) [x].[Name], [x].[Owner], [x].[Amount], [x].[CreationDate], [x].[BudgetId], [x].[UserId], CASE
    WHEN (
        SELECT CASE
            WHEN EXISTS (
                SELECT 1
                FROM [Expenses] AS [e]
                WHERE [x].[BudgetId] = [e].[UserBudgetBudgetId])

        END
    ) = 1

        SELECT SUM([y].[Amount])
        FROM [Expenses] AS [y]
        WHERE [x].[BudgetId] = [y].[UserBudgetBudgetId]
    ) ELSE 0E0
END AS [Balance]
FROM [Budgets] AS [x]
WHERE ([x].[BudgetId] = @__id_0) AND ([x].[IsDeleted] = 0)

SELECT TOP(2) [x].[Name], [x].[Owner], [x].[Amount], [x].[CreationDate], [x].[BudgetId], [x].[UserId], CASE
    WHEN (
        SELECT CASE
            WHEN EXISTS (
                SELECT 1
                FROM [Expenses] AS [e]
                WHERE [x].[BudgetId] = [e].[UserBudgetBudgetId])
            THEN CAST(1 AS BIT) ELSE CAST(0 AS BIT)
        END
    ) = 1
    THEN [x].[Amount] - (
        SELECT SUM([y].[Amount])
        FROM [Expenses] AS [y]
        WHERE [x].[BudgetId] = [y].[UserBudgetBudgetId]
    ) ELSE 0E0
END AS [Balance]
FROM [Budgets] AS [x]
WHERE ([x].[BudgetId] = @__id_0) AND ([x].[IsDeleted] = 0)
ORDER BY [x].[BudgetId]

2019-12-04 05:31:38.952 -06:00 [INF] Executed DbCommand (66ms) [Parameters=[@__id_0='32'], CommandType='"Text"', CommandTimeout='30']
SELECT TOP(2) [x].[Name], [x].[Owner], [x].[Amount], [x].[CreationDate], [x].[BudgetId], [x].[UserId], CASE
    WHEN (
        SELECT CASE
            WHEN EXISTS (
                SELECT 1
                FROM [Expenses] AS [e]
                WHERE [x].[BudgetId] = [e].[UserBudgetBudgetId])
            THEN CAST(1 AS BIT) ELSE CAST(0 AS BIT)
        END
    ) = 1
    THEN [x].[Amount] - (
        SELECT SUM([y].[Amount])
        FROM [Expenses] AS [y]
        WHERE [x].[BudgetId] = [y].[UserBudgetBudgetId]
    ) ELSE 0E0
END AS [Balance]
FROM [Budgets] AS [x]
WHERE ([x].[BudgetId] = @__id_0) AND ([x].[IsDeleted] = 0)
ORDER BY [x].[BudgetId]

FROM [Expenses] AS [x.Expenses]
INNER JOIN (

    FROM [Budgets] AS [x0]

) AS [t] ON [x.Expenses].[UserBudgetBudgetId] = [t].[BudgetId]
